<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stuntelig.html>stuntelig</a> (59072)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">stuntelen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bumble.html>bumble</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">-y</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stuurs.html>stuurs</a> (87642)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stuur.html>stuur</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:fierce.html>fierce</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:hostile.html>hostile</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-s</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos"><a href = vnd.unilang:adjectival.html>adjectival</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:suffix.html>suffix</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective"><a href = vnd.unilang:adjective.html>Adjective</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stuurs.html>stuurs</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stuurs.html>stuurser</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stuurs.html>stuurs</a></b> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a></i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">stuurst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>curmudgeonly, <a href = vnd.unilang:moody.html>moody</a>, dour, cranky</li></ol>
